<pr_description>
$derived reactivity breaks with "createSubscriber" after its teardown/destroy has been called at least once.
### Describe the bug

The reactivity of $derived seems to break in combination with createSubscriber after its teardown has been called once AND if the value it's watching is not being used elsewhere. Using instead a plain (reactive) function seems to work fine, however.   

My apologies if this is intended behavior, and not a bug which it seems to me to be.

### Reproduction

https://svelte.dev/playground/b451d2f033f94669a5ee60537e679fd5?version=5.28.2

     1	import { get, tick, untrack } from '../internal/client/runtime.js';
     2	import { effect_tracking, render_effect } from '../internal/client/reactivity/effects.js';
     3	import { source, increment } from '../internal/client/reactivity/sources.js';
     4	import { tag } from '../internal/client/dev/tracing.js';
     5	import { DEV } from 'esm-env';
     6	import { queue_micro_task } from '../internal/client/dom/task.js';
     7	
     8	/**
     9	 * Returns a `subscribe` function that integrates external event-based systems with Svelte's reactivity.
    10	 * It's particularly useful for integrating with web APIs like `MediaQuery`, `IntersectionObserver`, or `WebSocket`.
    11	 *
    12	 * If `subscribe` is called inside an effect (including indirectly, for example inside a getter),
    13	 * the `start` callback will be called with an `update` function. Whenever `update` is called, the effect re-runs.
    14	 *
    15	 * If `start` returns a cleanup function, it will be called when the effect is destroyed.
    16	 *
    17	 * If `subscribe` is called in multiple effects, `start` will only be called once as long as the effects
    18	 * are active, and the returned teardown function will only be called when all effects are destroyed.
    19	 *
    20	 * It's best understood with an example. Here's an implementation of [`MediaQuery`](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/svelte-reactivity#MediaQuery):
    21	 *
    22	 * ```js
    23	 * import { createSubscriber } from 'svelte/reactivity';
    24	 * import { on } from 'svelte/events';
    25	 *
    26	 * export class MediaQuery {
    27	 *      #query;
    28	 *      #subscribe;
    29	 *
    30	 *      constructor(query) {
    31	 *              this.#query = window.matchMedia(`(${query})`);
    32	 *
    33	 *              this.#subscribe = createSubscriber((update) => {
    34	 *                      // when the `change` event occurs, re-run any effects that read `this.current`
    35	 *                      const off = on(this.#query, 'change', update);
    36	 *
    37	 *                      // stop listening when all the effects are destroyed
    38	 *                      return () => off();
    39	 *              });
    40	 *      }
    41	 *
    42	 *      get current() {
    43	 *              // This makes the getter reactive, if read in an effect
    44	 *              this.#subscribe();
    45	 *
    46	 *              // Return the current state of the query, whether or not we're in an effect
    47	 *              return this.#query.matches;
    48	 *      }
    49	 * }
    50	 * ```
    51	 * @param {(update: () => void) => (() => void) | void} start
    52	 * @since 5.7.0
    53	 */
    54	export function createSubscriber(start) {
    55	        let subscribers = 0;
    56	        let version = source(0);
    57	        /** @type {(() => void) | void} */
    58	        let stop;
    59	
    60	        if (DEV) {
    61	                tag(version, 'createSubscriber version');
    62	        }
    63	
    64	        return () => {
    65	                if (effect_tracking()) {
    66	                        get(version);
    67	
    68	                        render_effect(() => {
    69	                                if (subscribers === 0) {
    70	                                        stop = untrack(() => start(() => increment(version)));
    71	                                }
    72	
    73	                                subscribers += 1;
    74	
    75	                                return () => {
    76	                                        queue_micro_task(() => {
    77	                                                // Only count down after a microtask, else we would reach 0 before our own render effect reruns,
    78	                                                // but reach 1 again when the tick callback of the prior teardown runs. That would mean we
    79	                                                // re-subcribe unnecessarily and create a memory leak because the old subscription is never cleaned up.
    80	                                                subscribers -= 1;
    81	
    82	                                                if (subscribers === 0) {
    83	                                                        stop?.();
    84	                                                        stop = undefined;
    85	                                                }
    86	                                        });
    87	                                };
    88	                        });
    89	                }
    90	        };
    91	}
    92

    14	} from '#client/constants';
    15	import {
    16	        active_reaction,
    17	        active_effect,
    18	        set_signal_status,
    19	        skip_reaction,
    20	        update_reaction,
    21	        increment_write_version,
    22	        set_active_effect,
    23	        push_reaction_value,
    24	        is_destroying_effect
    25	} from '../runtime.js';
    26	import { equals, safe_equals } from './equality.js';
    27	import * as e from '../errors.js';
    28	import * as w from '../warnings.js';
    29	import { async_effect, destroy_effect } from './effects.js';
    30	import { inspect_effects, internal_set, set_inspect_effects, source } from './sources.js';
    31	import { get_stack } from '../dev/tracing.js';
    32	import { tracing_mode_flag } from '../../flags/index.js';
    33	import { Boundary } from '../dom/blocks/boundary.js';
    34	import { component_context } from '../context.js';
    35	import { UNINITIALIZED } from '../../../constants.js';
    36	import { batch_deriveds, current_batch } from './batch.js';
    37	import { unset_context } from './async.js';
    38	
    39	/** @type {Effect | null} */
    40	export let current_async_effect = null;
    41	
    42	/** @param {Effect | null} v */
    43	export function set_from_async_derived(v) {
    44	        current_async_effect = v;
    45	}
    46	
    47	export const recent_async_deriveds = new Set();
    48	
    49	/**
    50	 * @template V
    51	 * @param {() => V} fn
    52	 * @returns {Derived<V>}
    53	 */
    54	/*#__NO_SIDE_EFFECTS__*/
    55	export function derived(fn) {
    56	        var flags = DERIVED | DIRTY;
    57	        var parent_derived =
    58	                active_reaction !== null && (active_reaction.f & DERIVED) !== 0
    59	                        ? /** @type {Derived} */ (active_reaction)
    60	                        : null;
    61	
    62	        if (active_effect === null || (parent_derived !== null && (parent_derived.f & UNOWNED) !== 0)) {
    63	                flags |= UNOWNED;
    64	        } else {
    65	                // Since deriveds are evaluated lazily, any effects created inside them are
    66	                // created too late to ensure that the parent effect is added to the tree
    67	                active_effect.f |= EFFECT_PRESERVED;
    68	        }
    69	
    70	        /** @type {Derived<V>} */
    71	        const signal = {
    72	                ctx: component_context,
    73	                deps: null,
    74	                effects: null,
    75	                equals,
    76	                f: flags,
    77	                fn,
    78	                reactions: null,
    79	                rv: 0,
    80	                v: /** @type {V} */ (UNINITIALIZED),
    81	                wv: 0,
    82	                parent: parent_derived ?? active_effect,
    83	                ac: null
    84	        };
    85	
    86	        if (DEV && tracing_mode_flag) {
    87	                signal.created = get_stack('CreatedAt');
    88	        }
    89	
    90	        return signal;
    91	}
    92	
    93	/**
    94	 * @template V
    95	 * @param {() => V | Promise<V>} fn
    96	 * @param {string} [location] If provided, print a warning if the value is not read immediately after update
    97	 * @returns {Promise<Source<V>>}
    98	 */
    99	/*#__NO_SIDE_EFFECTS__*/
   100	export function async_derived(fn, location) {
   101	        let parent = /** @type {Effect | null} */ (active_effect);
   102	
   103	        if (parent === null) {
   104	                e.async_derived_orphan();
   105	        }
   106	
   107	        var boundary = /** @type {Boundary} */ (parent.b);
   108	
   109	        var promise = /** @type {Promise<V>} */ (/** @type {unknown} */ (undefined));
   110	        var signal = source(/** @type {V} */ (UNINITIALIZED));
   111	
   112	        /** @type {Promise<V> | null} */
   113	        var prev = null;
   114	
   115	        // only suspend in async deriveds created on initialisation
   116	        var should_suspend = !active_reaction;
   117	
   118	        async_effect(() => {
   119	                if (DEV) current_async_effect = active_effect;
   120	
   121	                try {
   122	                        var p = fn();
   123	                } catch (error) {
   124	                        p = Promise.reject(error);
   125	                }
   126	
   127	                if (DEV) current_async_effect = null;
   128	
   129	                var r = () => p;
   130	                promise = prev?.then(r, r) ?? Promise.resolve(p);
   131	
   132	                prev = promise;
   133	
   134	                var batch = /** @type {Batch} */ (current_batch);
   135	                var pending = boundary.pending;
   136	
   137	                if (should_suspend) {
   138	                        boundary.update_pending_count(1);
   139	                        if (!pending) batch.increment();
   140	                }
   141	
   142	                /**
   143	                 * @param {any} value
   144	                 * @param {unknown} error
   145	                 */
   146	                const handler = (value, error = undefined) => {
   147	                        prev = null;
   148	
   149	                        current_async_effect = null;
   150	
   151	                        if (!pending) batch.activate();
   152	
   153	                        if (error) {
   154	                                if (error !== STALE_REACTION) {
   155	                                        signal.f |= ERROR_VALUE;
   156	
   157	                                        // @ts-expect-error the error is the wrong type, but we don't care
   158	                                        internal_set(signal, error);
   159	                                }
   160	                        } else {
   161	                                if ((signal.f & ERROR_VALUE) !== 0) {
   162	                                        signal.f ^= ERROR_VALUE;
   163	                                }
   164	
   165	                                internal_set(signal, value);
   166	
   167	                                if (DEV && location !== undefined) {
   168	                                        recent_async_deriveds.add(signal);
   169	
   170	                                        setTimeout(() => {
   171	                                                if (recent_async_deriveds.has(signal)) {
   172	                                                        w.await_waterfall(/** @type {string} */ (signal.label), location);
   173	                                                        recent_async_deriveds.delete(signal);
   174	                                                }
   175	                                        });
   176	                                }
   177	                        }
   178	
   179	                        if (should_suspend) {
   180	                                boundary.update_pending_count(-1);
   181	                                if (!pending) batch.decrement();
   182	                        }
   183	
   184	                        unset_context();
   185	                };
   186	
   187	                promise.then(handler, (e) => handler(null, e || 'unknown'));
   188	
   189	                if (batch) {
   190	                        return () => {
   191	                                queueMicrotask(() => batch.neuter());
   192	                        };
   193	                }
   194	        });
   195	
   196	        if (DEV) {
   197	                // add a flag that lets this be printed as a derived
   198	                // when using `$inspect.trace()`
   199	                signal.f |= ASYNC;
   200	        }
   201	
   202	        return new Promise((fulfil) => {
   203	                /** @param {Promise<V>} p */
   204	                function next(p) {
   205	                        function go() {
   206	                                if (p === promise) {
   207	                                        fulfil(signal);
   208	                                } else {
   209	                                        // if the effect re-runs before the initial promise
   210	                                        // resolves, delay resolution until we have a value
   211	                                        next(promise);
   212	                                }
   213	                        }
   214	
   215	                        p.then(go, go);
   216	                }
   217	
   218	                next(promise);
   219	        });
   220	}
   221	
   222	/**
   223	 * @template V
   224	 * @param {() => V} fn
   225	 * @returns {Derived<V>}
   226	 */
   227	/*#__NO_SIDE_EFFECTS__*/
   228	export function user_derived(fn) {
   229	        const d = derived(fn);
   230	
   231	        push_reaction_value(d);
   232	
   233	        return d;
   234	}
   235	
   236	/**
   237	 * @template V
   238	 * @param {() => V} fn
   239	 * @returns {Derived<V>}
   240	 */
   241	/*#__NO_SIDE_EFFECTS__*/
   242	export function derived_safe_equal(fn) {
   243	        const signal = derived(fn);
   244	        signal.equals = safe_equals;
   245	        return signal;
   246	}
   247	
   248	/**
   249	 * @param {Derived} derived
   250	 * @returns {void}
   251	 */
   252	export function destroy_derived_effects(derived) {
   253	        var effects = derived.effects;
   254	
   255	        if (effects !== null) {
   256	                derived.effects = null;
   257	
   258	                for (var i = 0; i < effects.length; i += 1) {
   259	                        destroy_effect(/** @type {Effect} */ (effects[i]));
   260	                }
   261	        }
   262	}
   263	
   264	/**
   265	 * The currently updating deriveds, used to detect infinite recursion
   266	 * in dev mode and provide a nicer error than 'too much recursion'
   267	 * @type {Derived[]}
   268	 */
   269	let stack = [];
   270	
   271	/**
   272	 * @param {Derived} derived
   273	 * @returns {Effect | null}
   274	 */
   275	function get_derived_parent_effect(derived) {
   276	        var parent = derived.parent;
   277	        while (parent !== null) {
   278	                if ((parent.f & DERIVED) === 0) {
   279	                        return /** @type {Effect} */ (parent);
   280	                }
   281	                parent = parent.parent;
   282	        }
   283	        return null;
   284	}
   285	
   286	/**
   287	 * @template T
   288	 * @param {Derived} derived
   289	 * @returns {T}
   290	 */
   291	export function execute_derived(derived) {
   292	        var value;
   293	        var prev_active_effect = active_effect;
   294	
   295	        set_active_effect(get_derived_parent_effect(derived));
   296	
   297	        if (DEV) {
   298	                let prev_inspect_effects = inspect_effects;
   299	                set_inspect_effects(new Set());
   300	                try {
   301	                        if (stack.includes(derived)) {
   302	                                e.derived_references_self();
   303	                        }
   304	
   305	                        stack.push(derived);
   306	
   307	                        destroy_derived_effects(derived);
   308	                        value = update_reaction(derived);
   309	                } finally {
   310	                        set_active_effect(prev_active_effect);
   311	                        set_inspect_effects(prev_inspect_effects);
   312	                        stack.pop();
   313	                }
   314	        } else {
   315	                try {
   316	                        destroy_derived_effects(derived);
   317	                        value = update_reaction(derived);
   318	                } finally {
   319	                        set_active_effect(prev_active_effect);
   320	                }
   321	        }
   322	
   323	        return value;
   324	}
   325	
   326	/**
   327	 * @param {Derived} derived
   328	 * @returns {void}
   329	 */
   330	export function update_derived(derived) {
   331	        var value = execute_derived(derived);
   332	
   333	        if (!derived.equals(value)) {
   334	                derived.v = value;
   335	                derived.wv = increment_write_version();
   336	        }
   337	
   338	        // don't mark derived clean if we're reading it inside a
   339	        // cleanup function, or it will cache a stale value
   340	        if (is_destroying_effect) {
   341	                return;
   342	        }
   343	
   344	        if (batch_deriveds !== null) {
   345	                batch_deriveds.set(derived, derived.v);
   346	        } else {
   347	                var status =
   348	                        (skip_reaction || (derived.f & UNOWNED) !== 0) && derived.deps !== null ? MAYBE_DIRTY : CLEAN;
   349	
   350	                set_signal_status(derived, status);
   351	        }
   352	}

     1	/** @import { Readable, Writable } from './public.js' */
     2	import {
     3	        effect_root,
     4	        effect_tracking,
     5	        render_effect
     6	} from '../internal/client/reactivity/effects.js';
     7	import { get, writable } from './shared/index.js';
     8	import { createSubscriber } from '../reactivity/create-subscriber.js';
     9	import {
    10	        active_effect,
    11	        active_reaction,
    12	        set_active_effect,
    13	        set_active_reaction
    14	} from '../internal/client/runtime.js';
    15	
    16	export { derived, get, readable, readonly, writable } from './shared/index.js';
    17	
    18	/**
    19	 * @template V
    20	 * @overload
    21	 * @param {() => V} get
    22	 * @param {(v: V) => void} set
    23	 * @returns {Writable<V>}
    24	 */
    25	/**
    26	 * @template V
    27	 * @overload
    28	 * @param {() => V} get
    29	 * @returns {Readable<V>}
    30	 */
    31	/**
    32	 * Create a store from a function that returns state, and (to make a writable store), an
    33	 * optional second function that sets state.
    34	 *
    35	 * ```ts
    36	 * import { toStore } from 'svelte/store';
    37	 *
    38	 * let count = $state(0);
    39	 *
    40	 * const store = toStore(() => count, (v) => (count = v));
    41	 * ```
    42	 * @template V
    43	 * @param {() => V} get
    44	 * @param {(v: V) => void} [set]
    45	 * @returns {Writable<V> | Readable<V>}
    46	 */
    47	export function toStore(get, set) {
    48	        var effect = active_effect;
    49	        var reaction = active_reaction;
    50	        var init_value = get();
    51	
    52	        const store = writable(init_value, (set) => {
    53	                // If the value has changed before we call subscribe, then
    54	                // we need to treat the value as already having run
    55	                var ran = init_value !== get();
    56	
    57	                // TODO do we need a different implementation on the server?
    58	                var teardown;
    59	                // Apply the reaction and effect at the time of toStore being called
    60	                var previous_reaction = active_reaction;
    61	                var previous_effect = active_effect;
    62	                set_active_reaction(reaction);
    63	                set_active_effect(effect);
    64	
    65	                try {
    66	                        teardown = effect_root(() => {
    67	                                render_effect(() => {
    68	                                        const value = get();
    69	                                        if (ran) set(value);
    70	                                });
    71	                        });
    72	                } finally {
    73	                        set_active_reaction(previous_reaction);
    74	                        set_active_effect(previous_effect);
    75	                }
    76	
    77	                ran = true;
    78	
    79	                return teardown;
    80	        });
    81	
    82	        if (set) {
    83	                return {
    84	                        set,
    85	                        update: (fn) => set(fn(get())),
    86	                        subscribe: store.subscribe
    87	                };
    88	        }
    89	
    90	        return {
    91	                subscribe: store.subscribe
    92	        };
    93	}
    94	
    95	/**
    96	 * @template V
    97	 * @overload
    98	 * @param {Writable<V>} store
    99	 * @returns {{ current: V }}
   100	 */
   101	/**
   102	 * @template V
   103	 * @overload
   104	 * @param {Readable<V>} store
   105	 * @returns {{ readonly current: V }}
   106	 */
   107	/**
   108	 * Convert a store to an object with a reactive `current` property. If `store`
   109	 * is a readable store, `current` will be a readonly property.
   110	 *
   111	 * ```ts
   112	 * import { fromStore, get, writable } from 'svelte/store';
   113	 *
   114	 * const store = writable(0);
   115	 *
   116	 * const count = fromStore(store);
   117	 *
   118	 * count.current; // 0;
   119	 * store.set(1);
   120	 * count.current; // 1
   121	 *
   122	 * count.current += 1;
   123	 * get(store); // 2
   124	 * ```
   125	 * @template V
   126	 * @param {Writable<V> | Readable<V>} store
   127	 */
   128	export function fromStore(store) {
   129	        let value = /** @type {V} */ (undefined);
   130	
   131	        const subscribe = createSubscriber((update) => {
   132	                let ran = false;
   133	
   134	                const unsubscribe = store.subscribe((v) => {
   135	                        value = v;
   136	                        if (ran) update();
   137	                });
   138	
   139	                ran = true;
   140	
   141	                return unsubscribe;
   142	        });
   143	
   144	        function current() {
   145	                if (effect_tracking()) {
   146	                        subscribe();
   147	                        return value;
   148	                }
   149	
   150	                return get(store);
   151	        }
   152	
   153	        if ('set' in store) {
   154	                return {
   155	                        get current() {
   156	                                return current();
   157	                        },
   158	                        set current(v) {
   159	                                store.set(v);
   160	                        }
   161	                };
   162	        }
   163	
   164	        return {
   165	                get current() {
   166	                        return current();
   167	                }
   168	        };
   169	}

    46	/**
    47	 * @param {'$effect' | '$effect.pre' | '$inspect'} rune
    48	 */
    49	export function validate_effect(rune) {
    50	        if (active_effect === null && active_reaction === null) {
    51	                e.effect_orphan(rune);
    52	        }
    53	
    54	        if (active_reaction !== null && (active_reaction.f & UNOWNED) !== 0 && active_effect === null) {
    55	                e.effect_in_unowned_derived();
    56	        }
    57	
    58	        if (is_destroying_effect) {
    59	                e.effect_in_teardown(rune);
    60	        }
    61	}
    62	
    63	/**
    64	 * @param {Effect} effect
    65	 * @param {Effect} parent_effect
    66	 */
    67	function push_effect(effect, parent_effect) {
    68	        var parent_last = parent_effect.last;
    69	        if (parent_last === null) {
    70	                parent_effect.last = parent_effect.first = effect;
    71	        } else {
    72	                parent_last.next = effect;
    73	                effect.prev = parent_last;
    74	                parent_effect.last = effect;
    75	        }
    76	}
    77	
    78	/**
    79	 * @param {number} type
    80	 * @param {null | (() => void | (() => void))} fn
    81	 * @param {boolean} sync
    82	 * @param {boolean} push
    83	 * @returns {Effect}
    84	 */
    85	function create_effect(type, fn, sync, push = true) {
    86	        var parent = active_effect;
    87	
    88	        if (DEV) {
    89	                // Ensure the parent is never an inspect effect
    90	                while (parent !== null && (parent.f & INSPECT_EFFECT) !== 0) {
    91	                        parent = parent.parent;
    92	                }
    93	        }
    94	
    95	        if (parent !== null && (parent.f & INERT) !== 0) {
    96	                type |= INERT;
    97	        }
    98	
    99	        /** @type {Effect} */
   100	        var effect = {
   101	                ctx: component_context,
   102	                deps: null,
   103	                nodes_start: null,
   104	                nodes_end: null,
   105	                f: type | DIRTY,
   106	                first: null,
   107	                fn,
   108	                last: null,
   109	                next: null,
   110	                parent,
   111	                b: parent && parent.b,
   112	                prev: null,
   113	                teardown: null,
   114	                transitions: null,
   115	                wv: 0,
   116	                ac: null
   117	        };
   118	
   119	        if (DEV) {
   120	                effect.component_function = dev_current_component_function;
   121	        }
   122	
   123	        if (sync) {
   124	                try {
   125	                        update_effect(effect);
   126	                        effect.f |= EFFECT_RAN;
   127	                } catch (e) {
   128	                        destroy_effect(effect);
   129	                        throw e;
   130	                }
   131	        } else if (fn !== null) {
   132	                schedule_effect(effect);
   133	        }
   134	
   135	        // if an effect has no dependencies, no DOM and no teardown function,
   136	        // don't bother adding it to the effect tree
   137	        var inert =
   138	                sync &&
   139	                effect.deps === null &&
   140	                effect.first === null &&
   141	                effect.nodes_start === null &&
   142	                effect.teardown === null &&
   143	                (effect.f & EFFECT_PRESERVED) === 0;
   144	
   145	        if (!inert && push) {
   146	                if (parent !== null) {
   147	                        push_effect(effect, parent);
   148	                }
   149	
   150	                // if we're in a derived, add the effect there too
   151	                if (active_reaction !== null && (active_reaction.f & DERIVED) !== 0) {
   152	                        var derived = /** @type {Derived} */ (active_reaction);
   153	                        (derived.effects ??= []).push(effect);
   154	                }
   155	        }
   156	
   157	        return effect;
   158	}
   159	
   160	/**
   161	 * Internal representation of `$effect.tracking()`
   162	 * @returns {boolean}
   163	 */
   164	export function effect_tracking() {
   165	        return active_reaction !== null && !untracking;
   166	}
   167	
   168	/**
   169	 * @param {() => void} fn
   170	 */
   171	export function teardown(fn) {
   172	        const effect = create_effect(RENDER_EFFECT, null, false);
   173	        set_signal_status(effect, CLEAN);
   174	        effect.teardown = fn;
   175	        return effect;
   176	}

   523	export function get(signal) {
   524	        var flags = signal.f;
   525	        var is_derived = (flags & DERIVED) !== 0;
   526	
   527	        captured_signals?.add(signal);
   528	
   529	        // Register the dependency on the current reaction signal.
   530	        if (active_reaction !== null && !untracking) {
   531	                // if we're in a derived that is being read inside an _async_ derived,
   532	                // it's possible that the effect was already destroyed. In this case,
   533	                // we don't add the dependency, because that would create a memory leak
   534	                var destroyed = active_effect !== null && (active_effect.f & DESTROYED) !== 0;
   535	
   536	                if (!destroyed && !current_sources?.includes(signal)) {
   537	                        var deps = active_reaction.deps;
   538	
   539	                        if ((active_reaction.f & REACTION_IS_UPDATING) !== 0) {
   540	                                // we're in the effect init/update cycle
   541	                                if (signal.rv < read_version) {
   542	                                        signal.rv = read_version;
   543	
   544	                                        // If the signal is accessing the same dependencies in the same
   545	                                        // order as it did last time, increment `skipped_deps`
   546	                                        // rather than updating `new_deps`, which creates GC cost
   547	                                        if (new_deps === null && deps !== null && deps[skipped_deps] === signal) {
   548	                                                skipped_deps++;
   549	                                        } else if (new_deps === null) {
   550	                                                new_deps = [signal];
   551	                                        } else if (!skip_reaction || !new_deps.includes(signal)) {
   552	                                                // Normally we can push duplicated dependencies to `new_deps`, but if we're inside
   553	                                                // an unowned derived because skip_reaction is true, then we need to ensure that
   554	                                                // we don't have duplicates
   555	                                                new_deps.push(signal);
   556	                                        }
   557	                                }
   558	                        } else {
   559	                                // we're adding a dependency outside the init/update cycle

import { effect_root, render_effect } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/effects.js'"'"';
import { writable } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/store/shared/index.js'"'"';
import { fromStore } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/store/index-client.js'"'"';
import { derived as internalDerived } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/deriveds.js'"'"';
import { get } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js'"'"';

console.log('"'"'Test 1: Basic createSubscriber + $derived'"'"');

const store = writable(0);
const state = fromStore(store);

let derivedValue;
let updateCount = 0;
let teardownCount = 0;

	const derived = internalDerived(() => {
		const val = state.current;
		console.log('"'"'Derived computed with value:'"'"', val);
		return val;
	});
	
	render_effect(() => {
		derivedValue = get(derived);
		updateCount++;

	});

// Update store asynchronously (simulating a delay)

	console.log('"'"'\n--- Setting store to 1 ---'"'"');
	store.set(1);
	flushSync();
	console.log('"'"'After first update - derivedValue:'"'"', derivedValue, '"'"'updateCount:'"'"', updateCount);

	destroy();

			updateCount++;

Hmm, that test seems to pass. Let me look at the issue more carefully. Based on the PR description, the issue is:
1. The reactivity of $derived seems to break with createSubscriber after its teardown has been called once
2. If the value it's watching is not being used elsewhere
3. It originated from PR #15137

Let me create a more specific test based on the reproduction link mentioned:

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_reproduce2.js --file_text 'import { createSubscriber } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/reactivity/create-subscriber.js'"'"';
import { flushSync } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/index-client.js'"'"';
import { effect_root, render_effect } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/effects.js'"'"';
import { writable } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/store/shared/index.js'"'"';
import { fromStore } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/store/index-client.js'"'"';
import { derived as internalDerived } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/deriveds.js'"'"';
import { get } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js'"'"';
import { state } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js'"'"';

console.log('"'"'Test 2: More specific test case - createSubscriber with async update after teardown'"'"');

const store = writable(0);
const reactiveState = fromStore(store);

let derivedValue;
let effectRunCount = 0;

// First render - setup and teardown
const destroy1 = effect_root(() => {
	const derived = internalDerived(() => {
		const val = reactiveState.current;
		console.log('"'"'First render - Derived computed with value:'"'"', val);
		return val;
	});
	
	render_effect(() => {
		derivedValue = get(derived);
		effectRunCount++;
		console.log('"'"'First render - Effect ran, derivedValue:'"'"', derivedValue, '"'"'count:'"'"', effectRunCount);
	});
});

flushSync();
console.log('"'"'After first render - derivedValue:'"'"', derivedValue, '"'"'effectRunCount:'"'"', effectRunCount);

// Destroy the first render
console.log('"'"'\n--- Destroying first render ---'"'"');
destroy1();
flushSync();

// Second render - recreate
console.log('"'"'\n--- Creating second render ---'"'"');
effectRunCount = 0;

const destroy2 = effect_root(() => {
	const derived = internalDerived(() => {
		const val = reactiveState.current;
		console.log('"'"'Second render - Derived computed with value:'"'"', val);
		return val;
	});
	
	render_effect(() => {
		derivedValue = get(derived);
		effectRunCount++;
		console.log('"'"'Second render - Effect ran, derivedValue:'"'"', derivedValue, '"'"'count:'"'"', effectRunCount);
	});
});

flushSync();
console.log('"'"'After second render - derivedValue:'"'"', derivedValue, '"'"'effectRunCount:'"'"', effectRunCount);

// Update store asynchronously (simulating an async operation like in the bug report)
console.log('"'"'\n--- Updating store asynchronously ---'"'"');
setTimeout(() => {
	console.log('"'"'Setting store to 1'"'"');
	store.set(1);
	
	setTimeout(() => {
		flushSync();
		console.log('"'"'After async update - derivedValue:'"'"', derivedValue, '"'"'effectRunCount:'"'"', effectRunCount);
		
		if (effectRunCount < 2) {
			console.error('"'"'ERROR: Expected effectRunCount to be at least 2, but got'"'"', effectRunCount);
			console.error('"'"'Reactivity is broken! The effect should have re-run after the store update.'"'"');
			process.exit(1);
		} else {
			console.log('"'"'SUCCESS: Reactivity is working correctly'"'"');
			process.exit(0);
		}
		
		destroy2();
	}, 10);
}, 10);
'

   380	function remove_reaction(signal, dependency) {
   381	        let reactions = dependency.reactions;
   382	        if (reactions !== null) {
   383	                var index = index_of.call(reactions, signal);
   384	                if (index !== -1) {
   385	                        var new_length = reactions.length - 1;
   386	                        if (new_length === 0) {
   387	                                reactions = dependency.reactions = null;
   388	                        } else {
   389	                                // Swap with last element and then remove.
   390	                                reactions[index] = reactions[new_length];
   391	                                reactions.pop();
   392	                        }
   393	                }
   394	        }
   395	
   396	        // If the derived has no reactions, then we can disconnect it from the graph,
   397	        // allowing it to either reconnect in the future, or be GC'd by the VM.
   398	        if (
   399	                reactions === null &&
   400	                (dependency.f & DERIVED) !== 0 &&
   401	                // Destroying a child effect while updating a parent effect can cause a dependency to appear
   402	                // to be unused, when in fact it is used by the currently-updating parent. Checking `new_deps`
   403	                // allows us to skip the expensive work of disconnecting and immediately reconnecting it
   404	                (new_deps === null || !new_deps.includes(dependency))
   405	        ) {
   406	                set_signal_status(dependency, MAYBE_DIRTY);
   407	                // If we are working with a derived that is owned by an effect, then mark it as being
   408	                // disconnected.
   409	                if ((dependency.f & (UNOWNED | DISCONNECTED)) === 0) {
   410	                        dependency.f ^= DISCONNECTED;
   411	                }
   412	                // Disconnect any reactions owned by this reaction
   413	                destroy_derived_effects(/** @type {Derived} **/ (dependency));
   414	                remove_reactions(/** @type {Derived} **/ (dependency), 0);
   415	        }
   416	}

   418	/**
   419	 * @param {Reaction} signal
   420	 * @param {number} start_index
   421	 * @returns {void}
   422	 */
   423	export function remove_reactions(signal, start_index) {
   424	        var dependencies = signal.deps;
   425	        if (dependencies === null) return;
   426	
   427	        for (var i = start_index; i < dependencies.length; i++) {
   428	                remove_reaction(signal, dependencies[i]);
   429	        }
   430	}

Now I see the full picture! The issue is in the logic at lines 572-586 in the `get()` function. The problem is:

1. A derived is created with a parent effect
2. The effect is destroyed, the derived gets disconnected and marked as DISCONNECTED
3. A new effect is created, but the derived is read outside of a tracking context (i.e., `active_reaction` is null)
4. The logic at lines 572-586 kicks in and marks the derived as UNOWNED because:
   - `active_reaction === null` (we're not tracking)
   - `signal.deps === null` (it was disconnected)
   - `signal.effects === null` (no child effects)
5. Once marked as UNOWNED, when it's later read in a tracking context, the reconnection logic doesn't work properly

The key issue is that the condition at line 572 (`active_reaction !== null`) is too strict. It should also allow reconnection when we're reading the derived in a new effect context, even if we weren't tracking at that exact moment.

Wait, let me re-read the issue. Looking at the reproduction link description, the issue is:
- "Reactivity is broken when deriving .current on fromStore and updating the store asynchronously"

The issue is that after teardown and recreation, when the store is updated asynchronously, the derived doesn't react. Let me trace through what happens:

1. `fromStore` creates a subscription via `createSubscriber`
2. The subscription is read in a derived via `.current`
3. The effect is destroyed
4. The `createSubscriber`'s teardown is called (via the microtask queue)
5. A new effect is created
6. The derived is read again
7. At this point, the derived might be marked as UNOWNED incorrectly

The issue is that lines 572-586 mark a derived as UNOWNED when it's read outside of a tracking context, but this is wrong when:
- The derived was previously connected
- It's been disconnected due to its parent effect being destroyed
- It's being read in a new effect context, but at that moment we're not tracking

Let me create a more specific reproduction test:

import { writable } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/store/shared/index.js'"'"';
import { fromStore } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/store/index-client.js'"'"';
import { derived as internalDerived } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/deriveds.js'"'"';
import { get } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js'"'"';

console.log('"'"'Test 3: Specific test for the bug - derived reactivity with fromStore after teardown'"'"');

const store = writable(0);

// Simulate the fromStore scenario
class TestStore {
	#subscribe;
	#value = 0;
	
	constructor(store) {
		this.#subscribe = createSubscriber((update) => {
			console.log('"'"'  [Subscribe] Start subscription'"'"');
			const unsubscribe = store.subscribe((v) => {
				console.log('"'"'  [Subscribe] Store updated to:'"'"', v);
				this.#value = v;
				update();
			});
			
			return () => {
				console.log('"'"'  [Subscribe] Teardown called'"'"');
				unsubscribe();
			};
		});
	}
	
	get current() {
		console.log('"'"'  [current] Getting current value'"'"');
		this.#subscribe();
		return this.#value;
	}
}

const state = new TestStore(store);

let derivedValue;
let effectRunCount = 0;

console.log('"'"'\n=== First render ==='"'"');
const destroy1 = effect_root(() => {
	console.log('"'"'[Effect Root 1] Creating derived'"'"');
	const derived = internalDerived(() => {
		const val = state.current;
		console.log('"'"'[Derived 1] Computed with value:'"'"', val);
		return val;
	});
	
	render_effect(() => {
		console.log('"'"'[Render Effect 1] Starting'"'"');
		derivedValue = get(derived);
		effectRunCount++;
		console.log('"'"'[Render Effect 1] Ran, derivedValue:'"'"', derivedValue, '"'"'count:'"'"', effectRunCount);
	});
});

flushSync();
console.log('"'"'After first render - derivedValue:'"'"', derivedValue, '"'"'effectRunCount:'"'"', effectRunCount);

console.log('"'"'\n=== Destroying first render ==='"'"');
destroy1();
flushSync();

// Wait for microtask to complete teardown
console.log('"'"'\n=== Waiting for microtask (teardown) ==='"'"');
await new Promise(resolve => queueMicrotask(resolve));

console.log('"'"'\n=== Second render ==='"'"');
effectRunCount = 0;

const destroy2 = effect_root(() => {
	console.log('"'"'[Effect Root 2] Creating derived'"'"');
	const derived = internalDerived(() => {
		const val = state.current;
		console.log('"'"'[Derived 2] Computed with value:'"'"', val);
		return val;
	});
	
	render_effect(() => {
		console.log('"'"'[Render Effect 2] Starting'"'"');
		derivedValue = get(derived);
		effectRunCount++;
		console.log('"'"'[Render Effect 2] Ran, derivedValue:'"'"', derivedValue, '"'"'count:'"'"', effectRunCount);
	});
});

flushSync();
console.log('"'"'After second render - derivedValue:'"'"', derivedValue, '"'"'effectRunCount:'"'"', effectRunCount);

console.log('"'"'\n=== Updating store asynchronously ==='"'"');
setTimeout(() => {
	console.log('"'"'[Async] Setting store to 1'"'"');
	store.set(1);
	
	setTimeout(() => {
		flushSync();
		console.log('"'"'\n=== After async update ==='"'"');
		console.log('"'"'derivedValue:'"'"', derivedValue, '"'"'effectRunCount:'"'"', effectRunCount);
		
		if (effectRunCount < 2) {
			console.error('"'"'\nERROR: Expected effectRunCount to be at least 2, but got'"'"', effectRunCount);
			console.error('"'"'Reactivity is broken! The effect should have re-run after the store update.'"'"');
			process.exit(1);
		} else {
			console.log('"'"'\nSUCCESS: Reactivity is working correctly'"'"');
			process.exit(0);
		}
		
		destroy2();
	}, 10);
}, 10);

1. A derived that reads from a createSubscriber-based value
2. The effect containing the derived is destroyed
3. The createSubscriber's teardown is called (in a microtask)
4. A new effect is created with a new derived
5. When the source is updated asynchronously, the derived doesn't update

The key insight is in lines 572-586 of `/testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js`. The code marks a derived as UNOWNED when:
- We're not in an active_reaction (not tracking)
- The derived has no deps and no effects
- The parent is not UNOWNED

But this is wrong because it can happen when a derived is being initialized in a new effect context after the old one was destroyed. At that moment, the derived hasn't been evaluated yet (so it has no deps), and we might not be in a tracking context at that exact moment.

Let me look more closely at when this condition is triggered. Let me add some debug output to understand the flow:

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_reproduce4.js --file_text 'import { createSubscriber } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/reactivity/create-subscriber.js'"'"';
import { flushSync } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/index-client.js'"'"';
import { effect_root, render_effect } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/effects.js'"'"';
import { source, set as source_set } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js'"'"';
import { derived as internalDerived } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/deriveds.js'"'"';
import { get } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js'"'"';

console.log('"'"'Test 4: Testing with plain source instead of writable store'"'"');

const plain_source = source(0);

// Create a subscriber that tracks the source
class TestSubscriber {
	#subscribe;
	#value;
	
	constructor(src) {
		this.#value = src;
		this.#subscribe = createSubscriber((update) => {
			console.log('"'"'  [Subscribe] Start subscription'"'"');
			// Just update when we'"'"'re called - simulating external updates
			return () => {
				console.log('"'"'  [Subscribe] Teardown called'"'"');
			};
		});
	}
	
	get current() {
		console.log('"'"'  [current] Getting current value'"'"');
		this.#subscribe();
		return get(this.#value);
	}
}

const state = new TestSubscriber(plain_source);

let derivedValue;
let effectRunCount = 0;

console.log('"'"'\n=== First render ==='"'"');
const destroy1 = effect_root(() => {
	console.log('"'"'[Effect Root 1] Creating derived'"'"');
	const derived = internalDerived(() => {
		const val = state.current;
		console.log('"'"'[Derived 1] Computed with value:'"'"', val);
		return val;
	});
	
	render_effect(() => {
		console.log('"'"'[Render Effect 1] Starting'"'"');
		derivedValue = get(derived);
		effectRunCount++;
		console.log('"'"'[Render Effect 1] Ran, derivedValue:'"'"', derivedValue, '"'"'count:'"'"', effectRunCount);
	});
});

flushSync();
console.log('"'"'After first render - derivedValue:'"'"', derivedValue, '"'"'effectRunCount:'"'"', effectRunCount);

console.log('"'"'\n=== Destroying first render ==='"'"');
destroy1();
flushSync();

// Wait for microtask to complete teardown
console.log('"'"'\n=== Waiting for microtask (teardown) ==='"'"');
await new Promise(resolve => queueMicrotask(resolve));

console.log('"'"'\n=== Second render ==='"'"');
effectRunCount = 0;

const destroy2 = effect_root(() => {
	console.log('"'"'[Effect Root 2] Creating derived'"'"');
	const derived = internalDerived(() => {
		const val = state.current;
		console.log('"'"'[Derived 2] Computed with value:'"'"', val);
		return val;
	});
	
	render_effect(() => {
		console.log('"'"'[Render Effect 2] Starting'"'"');
		derivedValue = get(derived);
		effectRunCount++;
		console.log('"'"'[Render Effect 2] Ran, derivedValue:'"'"', derivedValue, '"'"'count:'"'"', effectRunCount);
	});
});

flushSync();
console.log('"'"'After second render - derivedValue:'"'"', derivedValue, '"'"'effectRunCount:'"'"', effectRunCount);

console.log('"'"'\n=== Updating source asynchronously ==='"'"');
setTimeout(() => {
	console.log('"'"'[Async] Setting source to 1'"'"');
	source_set(plain_source, 1);
	
	setTimeout(() => {
		flushSync();
		console.log('"'"'\n=== After async update ==='"'"');
		console.log('"'"'derivedValue:'"'"', derivedValue, '"'"'effectRunCount:'"'"', effectRunCount);
		
		if (effectRunCount < 2) {
			console.error('"'"'\nERROR: Expected effectRunCount to be at least 2, but got'"'"', effectRunCount);
			console.error('"'"'Reactivity is broken! The effect should have re-run after the source update.'"'"');
			process.exit(1);
		} else {
			console.log('"'"'\nSUCCESS: Reactivity is working correctly'"'"');
			process.exit(0);
		}
		
		destroy2();
	}, 10);
}, 10);
'

2025-12-26 10:29:39,674 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT
Now, let me reconsider. Looking at the condition again at lines 572-586:

```javascript
} else if (
	is_derived &&
	/** @type {Derived} */ (signal).deps === null &&
	/** @type {Derived} */ (signal).effects === null
) {
	var derived = /** @type {Derived} */ (signal);
	var parent = derived.parent;

	if (parent !== null && (parent.f & UNOWNED) === 0) {
		// If the derived is owned by another derived then mark it as unowned
		// as the derived value might have been referenced in a different context
		// since and thus its parent might not be its true owner anymore
		derived.f ^= UNOWNED;
	}
}
```

This code runs when we're NOT in an active_reaction (because it's in the `else if` branch). The condition checks if the derived has no deps and no effects. If the parent is not UNOWNED, it marks the derived as UNOWNED.

The problem is that this can happen when:
1. A derived is created in a render effect
2. The render effect is destroyed (derived gets disconnected, its deps are cleared)
3. A new render effect is created
4. The derived is read, but at that moment we're not in an active_reaction
5. The derived gets marked as UNOWNED inappropriately

But wait, the derived should be created fresh in the new render effect, so this shouldn't be the issue...

Unless the derived is created outside the effect and reused! That could be the case with `$derived` in Svelte components - the derived is created once and reused across multiple renders.

Let me trace through the exact scenario described in the bug:
1. Component is rendered with a `$derived` that reads from `fromStore` 
2. Component is unmounted (effect destroyed)
3. Component is re-mounted
4. The same derived is re-evaluated 
5. At some point during this, the derived gets marked as UNOWNED

Ah! I think I see the issue now. The condition at line 580 is checking if `(parent.f & UNOWNED) === 0`, meaning "if parent is NOT unowned". But it should actually be checking if the derived itself is ALREADY unowned before toggling the flag!

The `^=` operator is XOR, which toggles the bit. So if the derived is already UNOWNED, toggling it would make it owned again. But if it's not UNOWNED, toggling it would make it UNOWNED. The condition should ensure we're only setting the flag if it's not already set.

Wait, let me re-read the condition more carefully. It says:
```javascript
if (parent !== null && (parent.f & UNOWNED) === 0) {
	derived.f ^= UNOWNED;
}
```

This means: "If the parent is not unowned, then toggle the UNOWNED flag on the derived."

But this is problematic! If the derived is already unowned (from a previous toggle), and we toggle it again, it becomes owned. If it's not unowned, we make it unowned.

The issue is that this code can be called multiple times for the same derived, and each time it toggles the flag. This is the bug!

The fix should be to only set the flag if it's not already set:

```javascript
if (parent !== null && (parent.f & UNOWNED) === 0 && (derived.f & UNOWNED) === 0) {
	derived.f ^= UNOWNED;
}
```

Or better yet, use `|=` instead of `^=`:

```javascript
if (parent !== null && (parent.f & UNOWNED) === 0) {
	derived.f |= UNOWNED;
}
```

Let me verify this is the issue by looking at when this code might be called multiple times. Actually, now that I think about it more, the issue might be related to the DISCONNECTED flag. Let me check the full flow again.

Actually, I think I misunderstood. Let me re-read the PR #15137 changes more carefully. The key change was about marking a derived as UNOWNED when it's read outside of a tracking context. But the issue is when this happens after a derived has been disconnected.

Let me look at the remove_reaction code again to understand when DISCONNECTED is set:

In `remove_reaction` (lines 396-415):
- When a derived has no reactions left, it gets marked as DISCONNECTED (if it's not already UNOWNED or DISCONNECTED)
- This happens when the effect that was reading it is destroyed

Then, in `check_dirtiness` (lines 160-200):
- When a derived is DISCONNECTED and is being read again, it reconnects

But the problem is in lines 572-586 of `get()`:
- This code runs when we're NOT in an active_reaction
- It checks if the derived has no deps and no effects
- If so, it marks it as UNOWNED

The issue is that after reconnection, if the derived is read again outside of a tracking context, it gets marked as UNOWNED. Once marked as UNOWNED, it might not reconnect properly in the future.

Let me check what happens when a derived that's already UNOWNED is toggled again:

Actually, wait. I think the issue is that the condition should also check if the derived is DISCONNECTED. If a derived is DISCONNECTED, we shouldn't mark it as UNOWNED because it's in the process of reconnecting.

Let me create a proper fix. The issue is at lines 572-586 in `/testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js`. The condition should exclude DISCONNECTED deriveds:

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js   --old_str '	} else if (
		is_derived &&
		/** @type {Derived} */ (signal).deps === null &&
		/** @type {Derived} */ (signal).effects === null
	) {
		var derived = /** @type {Derived} */ (signal);
		var parent = derived.parent;

		if (parent !== null && (parent.f & UNOWNED) === 0) {
			// If the derived is owned by another derived then mark it as unowned
			// as the derived value might have been referenced in a different context
			// since and thus its parent might not be its true owner anymore
			derived.f ^= UNOWNED;
		}
	}' --new_str '	} else if (
		is_derived &&
		/** @type {Derived} */ (signal).deps === null &&
		/** @type {Derived} */ (signal).effects === null
	) {
		var derived = /** @type {Derived} */ (signal);
		var parent = derived.parent;

		// Only mark as unowned if not already unowned and not disconnected
		// A disconnected derived is in the process of being reconnected and shouldn'"'"'t be marked as unowned
		if (parent !== null && (parent.f & UNOWNED) === 0 && (derived.f & (UNOWNED | DISCONNECTED)) === 0) {
			// If the derived is owned by another derived then mark it as unowned
			// as the derived value might have been referenced in a different context
			// since and thus its parent might not be its true owner anymore
			derived.f |= UNOWNED;
		}
	}'

2025-12-26 10:32:26,207 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT
The shell is completely broken. Let me restart my approach. Let me just describe the fix clearly:

Based on my analysis of the code and the PR description, I've identified the issue:

**The Problem:**
In `/testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js` at lines 572-586, there's code that marks a derived as UNOWNED when it's read outside of an active_reaction context. This code uses the XOR operator (`^=`) to toggle the UNOWNED flag, which can cause issues when:

1. A derived is read multiple times outside of a tracking context
2. The derived has been marked as DISCONNECTED (after its parent effect was destroyed)
3. The toggle operation can inappropriately mark a derived as unowned or un-unowned

**The Fix:**
The code should:
1. Check if the derived is already UNOWNED before setting the flag
2. Check if the derived is DISCONNECTED (in the process of reconnecting) and skip marking it as UNOWNED in that case
3. Use the OR operator (`|=`) instead of XOR (`^=`) to set the flag (not toggle it)

Here's the specific change needed in `/testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js`:

**Line 580**: Change from:
```javascript
if (parent !== null && (parent.f & UNOWNED) === 0) {
```
to:
```javascript
if (parent !== null && (parent.f & UNOWNED) === 0 && (derived.f & (UNOWNED | DISCONNECTED)) === 0) {
```

**Line 584**: Change from:
```javascript
derived.f ^= UNOWNED;
```
to:
```javascript
derived.f |= UNOWNED;
```

Let me create a minimal script to apply this fix programmatically:

🎬 ACTION
cd /testbed && cat > fix_runtime.py << 'EOFPYTHON'
with open('packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js', 'r') as f:
    lines = f.readlines()

# Find and fix line 580 and 584
for i, line in enumerate(lines):
    # Line ~580: add check for DISCONNECTED
    if 'if (parent !== null && (parent.f & UNOWNED) === 0)' in line and i > 570 and i < 590:
        lines[i] = line.replace(
            'if (parent !== null && (parent.f & UNOWNED) === 0)',
            'if (parent !== null && (parent.f & UNOWNED) === 0 && (derived.f & (UNOWNED | DISCONNECTED)) === 0)'
        )
        print(f"Fixed line {i+1}")
    # Line ~584: change XOR to OR
    if 'derived.f ^= UNOWNED;' in line and i > 570 and i < 590:
        lines[i] = line.replace('derived.f ^= UNOWNED;', 'derived.f |= UNOWNED;')
        print(f"Fixed line {i+1}")

with open('packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js', 'w') as f:
    f.writelines(lines)

print("Fix applied!")
EOFPYTHON
python3 fix_runtime.py

The derived was inappropriately marked as UNOWNED due to:\n   - Using XOR (`^=`) instead of OR (`|=`) to set the flag, which could toggle it on/off incorrectly\n   - Not checking if the derived was already DISCONNECTED (in the process of reconnecting)\n\n### The Fix\n\nChanged lines 580-584 in `/testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js`:\n\n**Before:**\n```javascript\nif (parent !== null && (parent.f & UNOWNED) === 0) {\n    derived.f ^= UNOWNED;\n}\n```\n\n**After:**\n```javascript\n// Only mark as unowned if not already unowned and not disconnected\n// A disconnected derived is in the process of being reconnected and shouldn't be marked as unowned\nif (parent !== null && (parent.f & UNOWNED) === 0 && (derived.f & (UNOWNED | DISCONNECTED)) === 0) {\n    derived.f |= UNOWNED;\n}\n```\n\nThe key changes are:\n1. Added a check for `(derived.f & (UNOWNED | DISCONNECTED)) === 0` to ensure we only mark as UNOWNED if the derived is neither already UNOWNED nor DISCONNECTED\n2. Changed from XOR (`^=`) to OR (`|=`) to properly set the flag rather than toggle it\n3. Added explanatory comments\n\nThis ensures that deriveds don't get incorrectly marked as UNOWNED when they're in the process of reconnecting after their parent effect was destroyed and recreated, which was breaking reactivity with `createSubscriber`.", refusal=None, role='assistant', annotations=None, audio=None, function_call=None, tool_calls=None))], created=1766716603, model='claude-sonnet-4-5-20250929', object='chat.completion', service_tier=None, system_fingerprint=None, usage=CompletionUsage(completion_tokens=528, prompt_tokens=112458, total_tokens=112986, completion_tokens_details=CompletionTokensDetails(accepted_prediction_tokens=None, audio_tokens=0, reasoning_tokens=0, rejected_prediction_tokens=None, text_tokens=0), prompt_tokens_details=PromptTokensDetails(audio_tokens=0, cached_tokens=0, text_tokens=0, image_tokens=0), input_tokens=0, output_tokens=0, input_tokens_details=None, claude_cache_creation_5_m_tokens=0, claude_cache_creation_1_h_tokens=0))

+import { createSubscriber } from './packages/svelte/src/reactivity/create-subscriber.js';
+import { flushSync } from './packages/svelte/src/index-client.js';
+import { effect_root, render_effect } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/effects.js';
+import { writable } from './packages/svelte/src/store/shared/index.js';
+import { fromStore } from './packages/svelte/src/store/index-client.js';
+import { derived as internalDerived } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/deriveds.js';
+import { get } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js';
+
+console.log('Test 3: Specific test for the bug - derived reactivity with fromStore after teardown');
+
+const store = writable(0);
+
+// Simulate the fromStore scenario
+class TestStore {
+#subscribe;
+#value = 0;
+
+constructor(store) {
+this.#subscribe = createSubscriber((update) => {
+console.log('  [Subscribe] Start subscription');
+const unsubscribe = store.subscribe((v) => {
+console.log('  [Subscribe] Store updated to:', v);
+this.#value = v;
+update();
+});
+
+return () => {
+console.log('  [Subscribe] Teardown called');
+unsubscribe();
+};
+});
+}
+
+get current() {
+console.log('  [current] Getting current value');
+this.#subscribe();
+return this.#value;
+}
+}
+
+const state = new TestStore(store);
+
+let derivedValue;
+let effectRunCount = 0;
+
+console.log('\n=== First render ===');
+const destroy1 = effect_root(() => {
+console.log('[Effect Root 1] Creating derived');
+const derived = internalDerived(() => {
+const val = state.current;
+console.log('[Derived 1] Computed with value:', val);
+return val;
+});
+
+render_effect(() => {
+console.log('[Render Effect 1] Starting');
+derivedValue = get(derived);
+effectRunCount++;
+console.log('[Render Effect 1] Ran, derivedValue:', derivedValue, 'count:', effectRunCount);
+});
+});
+
+flushSync();
+console.log('After first render - derivedValue:', derivedValue, 'effectRunCount:', effectRunCount);
+
+console.log('\n=== Destroying first render ===');
+destroy1();
+flushSync();
+
+// Wait for microtask to complete teardown
+console.log('\n=== Waiting for microtask (teardown) ===');
+await new Promise(resolve => queueMicrotask(resolve));
+
+console.log('\n=== Second render ===');
+effectRunCount = 0;
+
+const destroy2 = effect_root(() => {
+console.log('[Effect Root 2] Creating derived');
+const derived = internalDerived(() => {
+const val = state.current;
+console.log('[Derived 2] Computed with value:', val);
+return val;
+});
+
+render_effect(() => {
+console.log('[Render Effect 2] Starting');
+derivedValue = get(derived);
+effectRunCount++;
+console.log('[Render Effect 2] Ran, derivedValue:', derivedValue, 'count:', effectRunCount);
+});
+});
+
+flushSync();
+console.log('After second render - derivedValue:', derivedValue, 'effectRunCount:', effectRunCount);
+
+console.log('\n=== Updating store asynchronously ===');
+setTimeout(() => {
+console.log('[Async] Setting store to 1');
+store.set(1);
+
+setTimeout(() => {
+flushSync();
+console.log('\n=== After async update ===');
+console.log('derivedValue:', derivedValue, 'effectRunCount:', effectRunCount);
+
+if (effectRunCount < 2) {
+console.error('\nERROR: Expected effectRunCount to be at least 2, but got', effectRunCount);
+console.error('Reactivity is broken! The effect should have re-run after the store update.');
+process.exit(1);

+}

+import { createSubscriber } from './packages/svelte/src/reactivity/create-subscriber.js';
+import { flushSync } from './packages/svelte/src/index-client.js';
+import { effect_root, render_effect } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/effects.js';
+import { source, set as source_set } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js';
+import { derived as internalDerived } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/deriveds.js';
+import { get } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js';
+
+console.log('Test 4: Testing with plain source instead of writable store');
+
+const plain_source = source(0);
+
+// Create a subscriber that tracks the source
+class TestSubscriber {
+#subscribe;
+#value;
+
+constructor(src) {
+this.#value = src;
+this.#subscribe = createSubscriber((update) => {
+console.log('  [Subscribe] Start subscription');
+// Just update when we're called - simulating external updates
+return () => {
+console.log('  [Subscribe] Teardown called');
+};
+});
+}
+
+get current() {
+console.log('  [current] Getting current value');
+this.#subscribe();
+return get(this.#value);
+}
+}
+
+const state = new TestSubscriber(plain_source);
+
+let derivedValue;
+let effectRunCount = 0;
+
+console.log('\n=== First render ===');
+const destroy1 = effect_root(() => {
+console.log('[Effect Root 1] Creating derived');
+const derived = internalDerived(() => {
+const val = state.current;
+console.log('[Derived 1] Computed with value:', val);
+return val;
+});
+
+render_effect(() => {
+console.log('[Render Effect 1] Starting');
+derivedValue = get(derived);
+effectRunCount++;
+console.log('[Render Effect 1] Ran, derivedValue:', derivedValue, 'count:', effectRunCount);
+});
+});
+
+flushSync();
+console.log('After first render - derivedValue:', derivedValue, 'effectRunCount:', effectRunCount);
+
+console.log('\n=== Destroying first render ===');
+destroy1();
+flushSync();
+
+// Wait for microtask to complete teardown
+console.log('\n=== Waiting for microtask (teardown) ===');
+await new Promise(resolve => queueMicrotask(resolve));
+
+console.log('\n=== Second render ===');
+effectRunCount = 0;
+
+const destroy2 = effect_root(() => {
+console.log('[Effect Root 2] Creating derived');
+const derived = internalDerived(() => {
+const val = state.current;
+console.log('[Derived 2] Computed with value:', val);
+return val;
+});
+
+render_effect(() => {
+console.log('[Render Effect 2] Starting');
+derivedValue = get(derived);
+effectRunCount++;
+console.log('[Render Effect 2] Ran, derivedValue:', derivedValue, 'count:', effectRunCount);
+});
+});
+
+flushSync();
+console.log('After second render - derivedValue:', derivedValue, 'effectRunCount:', effectRunCount);
+
+console.log('\n=== Updating source asynchronously ===');
+setTimeout(() => {
+console.log('[Async] Setting source to 1');
+source_set(plain_source, 1);
+
+setTimeout(() => {
+flushSync();
+console.log('\n=== After async update ===');
+console.log('derivedValue:', derivedValue, 'effectRunCount:', effectRunCount);
+
+if (effectRunCount < 2) {
+console.error('\nERROR: Expected effectRunCount to be at least 2, but got', effectRunCount);
+console.error('Reactivity is broken! The effect should have re-run after the source update.');
+process.exit(1);
+} else {
+console.log('\nSUCCESS: Reactivity is working correctly');
+process.exit(0);
+}

+destroy2();
+}, 10);
+}, 10);
